/* version (SOCKS4) */\\n312:     socksreq[1] = 1; /* connect */\\n313:     socksreq[2] = (unsigned char)((sx->remote_port >> 8) & 0xff); /* MSB */\\n314:     socksreq[3] = (unsigned char)(sx->remote_port & 0xff); /* ensure empty userid is NUL-terminated */\\n403:     if(sx->proxy_user) {\\n404:       size_t plen = strlen(sx->proxy_user);\\n405:       if(plen >= (size_t)data->set.buffer_size - 8) {\\n406:         failf(data, \\\"Too long SOCKS proxy user name, can't use\\\");\\n407:         return CURLPX_LONG_USER;\\n408:       }\\n409:       /* copy the proxy name WITH trailing zero */\\n410:       memcpy(socksreq + 8, sx->proxy_user, plen + 1);\\n411:     }\\n412: \\n413:     /*\\n414:      * Make connection\\n415:      */\\n416:     {\\n417:       size_t packetsize = 9 +\\n418:         strlen((char *)socksreq + 8); CD is the result\\n483:    * code with one of the following values:\\n484:    *\\n485:    * 90: request granted\\n486:    * 91: request rejected or failed\\n487:    * 92: request rejected because SOCKS server cannot connect to\\n488:    *     identd on the client\\n489:    * 93: request rejected because the client program and identd\\n490:    *     report different user-ids\\n491:    */\\n492: \\n493:   /* wrong version ? */\\n494:   if(socksreq[0]) {\\n495:     failf(data,\\n496:           \\\"SOCKS4 reply has wrong version, version should be 0.\\\");\\n497:     return CURLPX_BAD_VERSION;\\n498:   }\\n499: \\n500:   /* Result */\\n501:   switch(socksreq[1]) {\\n502:   case 90:\\n503:     infof(data, \\\"SOCKS4%s request granted.\\\", protocol4a?\\\"a\\\":\\\"\\\");\\n504:     break;\\n505:   case 91:\\n506:     failf(data,\\n507:           \\\"Can't complete SOCKS4 connection to %d.%d.%d.%d:%d.               struct Curl_easy *data)\\n277: {\\n278:   struct connectdata *conn = cf->conn;\\n279:   const bool protocol4a =\\n280:     (conn->socks_proxy.proxytype == CURLPROXY_SOCKS4A) ? TRUE : FALSE;\\n281:   unsigned char *socksreq = (unsigned char *)data->state.buffer;\\n282:   CURLcode result;\\n283:   CURLproxycode presult;\\n284:   struct Curl_dns_entry *dns = NULL;\\n285: \\n286:   /* make sure that the buffer is at least 600 bytes */\\n287:   DEBUGASSERT(READBUFFER_MIN >= 600);\\n288: \\n289:   switch(sx->state) {\\n290:   case CONNECT_SOCKS_INIT:\\n291:     /* SOCKS4 can only do IPv4, insist! */\\n292:     conn->ip_version = CURL_IPRESOLVE_V4;\\n293:     if(conn->bits.httpproxy)\\n294:       infof(data, \\\"SOCKS4%s: connecting to HTTP proxy %s port %d\\\",\\n295:             protocol4a ? \\\"a\\\" : \\\"\\\", sx->hostname, sx->remote_port);\\n296: \\n297:     infof(data, \\\"SOCKS4 communication to %s:%d\\\",\\n298:           sx->hostname, sx->remote_port);\\n299: \\n300:     /*\\n301:      * Compose socks4 request\\n302:      *\\n303:      * Request format\\n304:      *\\n305:      *     +----+----+----+----+----+----+----+----+----+----+....+----+\\n306:      *     | VN | CD | DSTPORT |      DSTIP        | USERID       |NULL|\\n307:      *     +----+----+----+----+----+----+----+----+----+----+....+----+\\n308:      * # of bytes:  1    1      2              4           variable       1\\n309:      */\\n310: \\n311:     socksreq[0] = 4; /* version (SOCKS4) */\\n312:     socksreq[1] = 1; /* connect */\\n313:     socksreq[2] = (unsigned char)((sx->remote_port >> 8) & 0xff); /* MSB */\\n314:     socksreq[3] = (unsigned char)(sx->remote_port & 0xff);        /* LSB */\\n315: \\n316:     /* DNS resolve only for SOCKS4, not SOCKS4a */\\n317:     if(!protocol4a) {\\n318:       enum resolve_t rc =\\n319:         Curl_resolv(data, sx->hostname, sx->remote_port, TRUE, &dns);\\n320: \\n321:       if(rc == CURLRESOLV_ERROR)\\n322:         return CURLPX_RESOLVE_HOST;\\n323:       else if(rc == CURLRESOLV_PENDING) {\\n324:         sxstate(sx, data, CONNECT_RESOLVING);\\n325:         infof(data, \\\"SOCKS4 non-blocking resolve of %s\\\", sx->hostname);\\n326:         return CURLPX_OK;\\n327:       }\\n328:       sxstate(sx, data, CONNECT_RESOLVED);\\n329:       goto CONNECT_RESOLVED;\\n330:     }\\n331: \\n332:     /* socks4a doesn't resolve anything locally */\\n333:     sxstate(sx, data, CONNECT_REQ_INIT);\\n334:     goto CONNECT_REQ_INIT;\\n335: \\n336:   case CONNECT_RESOLVING:\\n337:     /* check if we have the name resolved by now */\\n338:     dns = Curl_fetch_addr(data, sx->hostname, (int)conn->port);\\n339: \\n340:     if(dns) {\\n341: #ifdef CURLRES_ASYNCH\\n342:       data->state.async.dns = dns;\\n343:       data->state.async.done = TRUE;\\n344: #endif\\n345:       infof(data, \\\"Hostname '%s' was found\\\", sx->hostname);\\n346:       sxstate(sx, data, CONNECT_RESOLVED);\\n347:     }\\n348:     else {\\n349:       result = Curl_resolv_check(data, &dns);\\n350:       if(!dns) {\\n351:         if(result)\\n352:           return CURLPX_RESOLVE_HOST;\\n353:         return CURLPX_OK;\\n354:       }\\n355:     }\\n356:     /* FALLTHROUGH */\\n357: CONNECT_RESOLVED:\\n358:   case CONNECT_RESOLVED: {\\n359:     struct Curl_addrinfo *hp = NULL;\\n360:     /*\\n361:      * We cannot use 'hostent' as a struct that Curl_resolv() returns.  It\\n362:      * returns a Curl_addrinfo pointer that may not always look the same.\\n363:      */\\n364:     if(dns) {\\n365:       hp = dns->addr;\\n366: \\n367:       /* scan for the first IPv4 address */\\n368:       while(hp && (hp->ai_family != AF_INET))\\n369:         hp = hp->ai_next;\\n370: \\n371:       if(hp) {\\n372:         struct sockaddr_in *saddr_in;\\n373:         char buf[64];\\n374:         Curl_printable_address(hp, buf, sizeof(buf));\\n375: \\n376:         saddr_in = (struct sockaddr_in *)(void *)hp->ai_addr;\\n377:         socksreq[4] = ((unsigned char *)&saddr_in->sin_addr.s_addr)[0];\\n378:         socksreq[5] = ((unsigned char *)&saddr_in->sin_addr.s_addr)[1];\\n379:         socksreq[6] = ((unsigned char *)&saddr_in->sin_addr.s_addr)[2];\\n380:         socksreq[7] = ((unsigned char *)&saddr_in->sin_addr.s_addr)[3];\\n381: \\n382:         infof(data, \\\"SOCKS4 connect to IPv4 %s (locally resolved)\\\", buf);\\n383: \\n384:         Curl_resolv_unlock(data, dns); /* not used anymore from now on */\\n385:       }\\n386:       else\\n387:         failf(data, \\\"SOCKS4 connection to %s not supported\\\", sx->hostname);\\n388:     }\\n389:     else\\n390:       failf(data, \\\"Failed to resolve \\\\\\\"%s\\\\\\\" for SOCKS4 connect.\\\",\\n391:             sx->hostname);\\n392: \\n393:     if(!hp)\\n394:       return CURLPX_RESOLVE_HOST;\\n395:   }\\n396:     /* FALLTHROUGH */\\n397: CONNECT_REQ_INIT:\\n398:   case CONNECT_REQ_INIT:\\n399:     /*\\n400:      * This is currently not supporting \\\"Identification Protocol (RFC1413)\\\".\\n401:      */\\n402:     socksreq[8] = 0; /* ensure empty userid is NUL-terminated */\\n403:     if(sx->proxy_user) {\\n404:       size_t plen = strlen(sx->proxy_user);\\n405:       if(plen >= (size_t)data->set.buffer_size - 8) {\\n406:         failf(data, \\\"Too long SOCKS proxy user name, can't use\\\");\\n407:         return CURLPX_LONG_USER;\\n408:       }\\n409:       /* copy the proxy name WITH trailing zero */\\n410:       memcpy(socksreq + 8, sx->proxy_user, plen + 1);\\n411:     }\\n412: \\n413:     /*\\n414:      * Make connection\\n415:      */\\n416:     {\\n417:       size_t packetsize = 9 +\\n418:         strlen((char *)socksreq + 8); /* size including NUL */\\n419: \\n420:       /* If SOCKS4a, set special invalid IP address 0.0.0.x */\\n421:       if(protocol4a) {\\n422:         size_t hostnamelen = 0;\\n423:         socksreq[4] = 0;\\n424:         socksreq[5] = 0;\\n425:         socksreq[6] = 0;\\n426:         socksreq[7] = 1;\\n427:         /* append hostname */\\n428:         hostnamelen = strlen(sx->hostname) + 1; /* length including NUL */\\n429:         if(hostnamelen <= 255)\\n430:           strcpy((char *)socksreq + packetsize, sx->hostname);\\n431:         else {\\n432:           failf(data, \\\"SOCKS4: too long host name\\\");\\n433:           return CURLPX_LONG_HOSTNAME;\\n434:         }\\n435:         packetsize += hostnamelen;\\n436:       }\\n437:       sx->outp = socksreq;\\n438:       sx->outstanding = packetsize;\\n439:       sxstate(sx, data, CONNECT_REQ_SENDING);\\n440:     }\\n441:     /* FALLTHROUGH */\\n442:   case CONNECT_REQ_SENDING:\\n443:     /* Send request */\\n444:     presult = socks_state_send(cf, sx, data, CURLPX_SEND_CONNECT,\\n445:                                \\\"SOCKS4 connect request\\\");\\n446:     if(CURLPX_OK != presult)\\n447:       return presult;\\n448:     else if(sx->outstanding) {\\n449:       /* remain in sending state */\\n450:       return CURLPX_OK;\\n451:     }\\n452:     /* done sending! */\\n453:     sx->outstanding = 8; CD is the result\\n483:    * code with one of the following values:\\n484:    *\\n485:    * 90: request granted\\n486:    * 91: request rejected or failed\\n487:    * 92: request rejected because SOCKS server cannot connect to\\n488:    *     identd on the client\\n489:    * 93: request rejected because the client program and identd\\n490:    *     report different user-ids\\n491:    */\\n492: \\n493:   /* wrong version ? */\\n494:   if(socksreq[0]) {\\n495:     failf(data,\\n496:           \\\"SOCKS4 reply has wrong version, version should be 0.\\\");\\n497:     return CURLPX_BAD_VERSION;\\n498:   }\\n499: \\n500:   /* Result */\\n501:   switch(socksreq[1]) {\\n502:   case 90:\\n503:     infof(data, \\\"SOCKS4%s request granted.\\\", protocol4a?\\\"a\\\":\\\"\\\");\\n504:     break;\\n505:   case 91:\\n506:     failf(data,\\n507:           \\\"Can't complete SOCKS4 connection to %d.%d.%d.%d:%d. (%d)\\\"\\n508:           \\\", request rejected or failed.\\\",\\n509:           socksreq[4], socksreq[5], socksreq[6], socksreq[7],\\n510:           (((unsigned char)socksreq[2] << 8) | (unsigned char)socksreq[3]),\\n511:           (unsigned char)socksreq[1]);\\n512:     return CURLPX_REQUEST_FAILED;\\n513:   case 92:\\n514:     failf(data,\\n515:           \\\"Can't complete SOCKS4 connection to %d.%d.%d.%d:%d. (%d)\\\"\\n516:           \\\", request rejected because SOCKS server cannot connect to \\\"\\n517:           \\\"identd on the client.\\\",\\n518:           socksreq[4], socksreq[5], socksreq[6], socksreq[7],\\n519:           (((unsigned char)socksreq[2] << 8) | (unsigned char)socksreq[3]),\\n520:           (unsigned char)socksreq[1]);\\n521:     return CURLPX_IDENTD;\\n522:   case 93:\\n523:     failf(data,\\n524:           \\\"Can't complete SOCKS4 connection to %d.%d.%d.%d:%d. (%d)\\\"\\n525:           \\\", request rejected because the client program and identd \\\"\\n526:           \\\"report different user-ids.\\\",\\n527:           socksreq[4], socksreq[5], socksreq[6], socksreq[7],\\n528:           (((unsigned char)socksreq[2] << 8) | (unsigned char)socksreq[3]),\\n529:           (unsigned char)socksreq[1]);\\n530:     return CURLPX_IDENTD_DIFFER;\\n531:   default:\\n532:     failf(data,\\n533:           \\\"Can't complete SOCKS4 connection to %d.%d.%d.%d:%d. (%d)\\\"\\n534:           \\\", Unknown.\\\",\\n535:           socksreq[4], socksreq[5], socksreq[6], socksreq[7],\\n536:           (((unsigned char)socksreq[2] << 8) | (unsigned char)socksreq[3]),\\n537:           (unsigned char)socksreq[1]);\\n538:     return CURLPX_UNKNOWN_FAIL;\\n539:   }\\n540: \\n541:   return CURLPX_OK; /* Proxy was successful! */\\n542: }\\n543: \\n544: /*\\n545:  * This function logs in to a SOCKS5 proxy and sends the specifics to the final\\n546:  * destination server.\\n547:  */\\n548: static CURLproxycode do_SOCKS5(struct Curl_cfilter *cf,\\n549:                                struct socks_state *sx,\\n550:                                struct Curl_easy *data)\\n551: {\\n552:   /*\\n553:     According to the RFC1928, section \\\"6.  Replies\\\". This is what a SOCK5\\n554:     replies:\\n555: \\n556:         +----+-----+-------+------+----------+----------+\\n557:         |VER | REP |  RSV  | ATYP | BND.ADDR | BND.PORT |\\n558:         +----+-----+-------+------+----------+----------+\\n559:         | 1  |  1  | X'00' |  1   | Variable |    2     |\\n560:         +----+-----+-------+------+----------+----------+\\n561: \\n562:     Where:\\n563: \\n564:     o  VER    protocol version: X'05'\\n565:     o  REP    Reply field:\\n566:     o  X'00' succeeded\\n567:   */\\n568:   struct connectdata *conn = cf->conn;\\n569:   unsigned char *socksreq = (unsigned char *)data->state.buffer;\\n570:   int idx;\\n571:   CURLcode result;\\n572:   CURLproxycode presult;\\n573:   bool socks5_resolve_local =\\n574:     (conn->socks_proxy.proxytype == CURLPROXY_SOCKS5) ?   /* version */\\n609:     idx++;                 /* number of authentication methods */\\n610:     socksreq[idx++] = 0;   /* no authentication */\\n611:     if(allow_gssapi)\\n612:       socksreq[idx++] = 1; /* GSS-API */\\n613:     if(sx->proxy_user)\\n614:       socksreq[idx++] = 2; /* username/password */\\n615:     /* write the number of authentication methods */\\n616:     socksreq[1] = (unsigned char) (idx - 2);\\n617: \\n618:     sx->outp = socksreq;\\n619:     sx->outstanding = idx;\\n620:     presult = socks_state_send(cf, sx, data, CURLPX_SEND_CONNECT,\\n621:                                \\\"initial SOCKS5 request\\\");\\n622:     if(CURLPX_OK != presult)\\n623:       return presult;\\n624:     else if(sx->outstanding) {\\n625:       /* remain in sending state */\\n626:       return CURLPX_OK;\\n627:     }\\n628:     sxstate(sx, data, CONNECT_SOCKS_READ);\\n629:     goto CONNECT_SOCKS_READ_INIT;\\n630:   case CONNECT_SOCKS_SEND:\\n631:     presult = socks_state_send(cf, sx, data, CURLPX_SEND_CONNECT,\\n632:                                \\\"initial SOCKS5 request\\\");\\n633:     if(CURLPX_OK != presult)\\n634:       return presult;\\n635:     else if(sx->outstanding) {\\n636:       /* remain in sending state */\\n637:       return CURLPX_OK;\\n638:     }\\n639:     /* FALLTHROUGH */\\n640: CONNECT_SOCKS_READ_INIT:\\n641:   case CONNECT_SOCKS_READ_INIT:\\n642:     sx->outstanding = 2; /* expect two bytes */\\n643:     sx->outp = socksreq; /* store it here */\\n644:     /* FALLTHROUGH */\\n645:   case CONNECT_SOCKS_READ:\\n646:     presult = socks_state_recv(cf, sx, data, CURLPX_RECV_CONNECT,\\n647:                                \\\"initial SOCKS5 response\\\");\\n648:     if(CURLPX_OK != presult)\\n649:       return presult;\\n650:     else if(sx->outstanding) {\\n651:       /* remain in reading state */\\n652:       return CURLPX_OK;\\n653:     }\\n654:     else if(socksreq[0] != 5) {\\n655:       failf(data, \\\"Received invalid version in initial SOCKS5 response.\\\");\\n656:       return CURLPX_BAD_VERSION;\\n657:     }\\n658:     else if(socksreq[1] == 0) {\\n659:       /* DONE! No authentication needed. if(!allow_gssapi && (socksreq[1] == 1)) {\\n681:         failf(data,\\n682:               \\\"SOCKS5 GSSAPI per-message authentication is not supported.\\\");\\n683:         return CURLPX_GSSAPI_PERMSG;\\n684:       }\\n685:       else if(socksreq[1] == 255) {\\n686:         failf(data, \\\"No authentication method was acceptable.\\\");\\n687:         return nothing! */\\n700:     break;\\n701: \\n702: CONNECT_AUTH_INIT:\\n703:   case CONNECT_AUTH_INIT: {\\n704:     /* Needs user name and password */\\n705:     size_t proxy_user_len, }\\n710:     else {\\n711:       proxy_user_len = 0;\\n712:       proxy_password_len = 0;\\n713:     }\\n714: \\n715:     /*   username/password request looks like\\n716:      * socksreq[len++] = (unsigned char) proxy_user_len;\\n725:     if(sx->proxy_user && proxy_user_len) {\\n726:       /* the length must fit in a single byte */\\n727:       if(proxy_user_len > 255) /* the length must fit in a single byte */\\n737:       if(proxy_password_len > 255) {\\n738:         failf(data, \\\"Excessive password length for proxy auth\\\");\\n739:         return CURLPX_LONG_PASSWD;\\n740:       }\\n741:       memcpy(socksreq + len, sx->proxy_password, proxy_password_len);\\n742:     }\\n743:     len += proxy_password_len;\\n744:     sxstate(sx, data, CONNECT_AUTH_SEND);\\n745:     sx->outstanding = len;\\n746:     sx->outp = socksreq;\\n747:   }\\n748:     /* FALLTHROUGH */\\n749:   case CONNECT_AUTH_SEND:\\n750:     presult = socks_state_send(cf, sx, data, CURLPX_SEND_AUTH,\\n751:                                \\\"SOCKS5 sub-negotiation request\\\");\\n752:     if(CURLPX_OK != presult)\\n753:       return presult;\\n754:     else if(sx->outstanding) {\\n755:       /* remain in sending state */\\n756:       return CURLPX_OK;\\n757:     }\\n758:     sx->outp = socksreq;\\n759:     sx->outstanding = 2;\\n760:     sxstate(sx,  if(err) {\n123:         break;\n124:       }\n125:     }\n126: \n127:     if(buffersize == nread) {\n128:       allread += nread;\n129:       *n = allread;\n130:       result = CURLE_OK;\n131:       break;\n132:     }\n133:     if(!nread) {\n134:       result = ~CURLE_OK;\n135:       break;\n136:     }\n137: \n138:     buffersize -= nread;\n139:     buf += nread;\n140:     allread += nread;\n141:   }\n142:   return result;\n143: }\n144: #endif\n145: \n146: #if defined(DEBUGBUILD) && !defined(CURL_DISABLE_VERBOSE_STRINGS)\n147: #define DEBUG_AND_VERBOSE\n148: #define sxstate(x,d,y) socksstate(x,d,y, __LINE__)\n149: #else\n150: #define sxstate(x,d,y) socksstate(x,d,y)\n151: #endif\n152: \n153: /* always use this function to change state, to make debugging easier */\n154: static void socksstate(struct socks_state *sx, struct Curl_easy *data,\n155:                        enum connect_t state\n156: #ifdef DEBUG_AND_VERBOSE\n157:                        , int lineno\n158: #endif\n159: )\n160: {\n161:   enum connect_t oldstate = sx->state;\n162: #ifdef DEBUG_AND_VERBOSE\n163:   /* synced with the state list in urldata.h */\n164:   static const char * const socks_statename[] = {\n165:     \"INIT\",\n166:     \"SOCKS_INIT\",\n167:     \"SOCKS_SEND\",\n168:     \"SOCKS_READ_INIT\",\n169:     \"SOCKS_READ\",\n170:     \"GSSAPI_INIT\",\n171:     \"AUTH_INIT\",\n172:     \"AUTH_SEND\",\n173:     \"AUTH_READ\",\n174:     \"REQ_INIT\",\n175:     \"RESOLVING\",\n176:     \"RESOLVED\",\n177:     \"RESOLVE_REMOTE\",\n178:     \"REQ_SEND\",\n179:     \"REQ_SENDING\",\n180:     \"REQ_READ\",\n181:     \"REQ_READ_MORE\",\n182:     \"DONE\"\n183:   };\n184: #endif\n185: \n186:   (void)data;\n187:   if(oldstate == state)\n188:     /* don't bother when the new state is the same as the old state */\n189:     return;\n190: \n191:   sx->state = state;\n192: \n193: #ifdef DEBUG_AND_VERBOSE\n194:   infof(data,\n195:         \"SXSTATE: %s => %s; line %d\",\n196:         socks_statename[oldstate], socks_statename[sx->state],\n197:         lineno);\n198: #endif\n199: }\n200: \n201: static CURLproxycode socks_state_send(struct Curl_cfilter *cf,\n202:                                       struct socks_state *sx,\n203:                                       struct Curl_easy *data,\n204:                                       CURLproxycode failcode,\n205:                                       const char *description)\n206: {\n207:   ssize_t nwritten;\n208:   CURLcode result;\n209: \n210:   nwritten = Curl_conn_cf_send(cf->next, data, (char *)sx->outp,\n211:                                sx->outstanding, &result);\n212:   if(nwritten <= 0) {\n213:     if(CURLE_AGAIN == result) {\n214:       return CURLPX_OK;\n215:     }\n216:     else if(CURLE_OK == result) {\n217:       /* connection closed */\n218:       failf(data, \"connection to proxy closed\");\n219:       return CURLPX_CLOSED;\n220:     }\n221:     failf(data, \"Failed to send %s: %s\", description,\n222:           curl_easy_strerror(result));\n223:     return failcode;\n224:   }\n225:   DEBUGASSERT(sx->outstanding >= nwritten);\n226:   /* not done, remain in state */\n227:   sx->outstanding -= nwritten;\n228:   sx->outp += nwritten;\n229:   return CURLPX_OK;\n230: }\n231: \n232: static CURLproxycode socks_state_recv(struct Curl_cfilter *cf,\n233:                                       struct socks_state *sx,\n234:                                       struct Curl_easy *data,\n235:                                       CURLproxycode failcode,\n236:                                       const char *description)\n237: {\n238:   ssize_t nread;\n239:   CURLcode result;\n240: \n241:   nread = Curl_conn_cf_recv(cf->next, data, (char *)sx->outp,\n242:                             sx->outstanding, &result);\n243:   if(nread <= 0) {\n244:     if(CURLE_AGAIN == result) {\n245:       return CURLPX_OK;\n246:     }\n247:     else if(CURLE_OK == result) {\n248:       /* connection closed */\n249:       failf(data, \"connection to proxy closed\");\n250:       return CURLPX_CLOSED;\n251:     }\n252:     failf(data, \"SOCKS4: Failed receiving %s: %s\", description,\n253:           curl_easy_strerror(result));\n254:     return failcode;\n255:   }\n256:   /* remain in reading state */\n257:   DEBUGASSERT(sx->outstanding >= nread);\n258:   sx->outstanding -= nread;\n259:   sx->outp += nread;\n260:   return CURLPX_OK;\n261: }\n262: \n263: /*\n264: * This function logs in to a SOCKS4 proxy and sends the specifics to the final\n265: * destination server.\n266: *\n267: * Reference :\n268: *   https://www.openssh.com/txt/socks4.protocol\n269: *\n270: * Note :\n271: *   Set protocol4a=true for  \"SOCKS 4A (Simple Extension to SOCKS 4 Protocol)\"\n272: *   Nonsupport \"Identification Protocol (RFC1413)\"\n273: */\n274: static CURLproxycode do_SOCKS4(struct Curl_cfilter *cf,\n275:                                struct socks_state *sx,\n276:                                struct Curl_easy *data)\n277: {\n278:   struct connectdata *conn = cf->conn;\n279:   const bool protocol4a =\n280:     (conn->socks_proxy.proxytype == CURLPROXY_SOCKS4A) ? TRUE : FALSE;\n281:   unsigned char *socksreq = (unsigned char *)data->state.buffer;\n282:   CURLcode result;\n283:   CURLproxycode presult;\n284:   struct Curl_dns_entry *dns = NULL;\n285: \n286:   /* make sure that the buffer is at least 600 bytes */\n287:   DEBUGASSERT(READBUFFER_MIN >= 600);\n288: \n289:   switch(sx->state) {\n290:   case CONNECT_SOCKS_INIT:\n291:     /* SOCKS4 can only do IPv4, insist! */\n292:     conn->ip_version = CURL_IPRESOLVE_V4;\n293:     if(conn->bits.httpproxy)\n294:       infof(data, \"SOCKS4%s: connecting to HTTP proxy %s port %d\",\n295:             protocol4a ? \"a\" : \"\", sx->hostname, sx->remote_port);\n296: \n297:     infof(data, \"SOCKS4 communication to %s:%d\",\n298:           sx->hostname, sx->remote_port);\n299: \n300:     /*\n301:      * Compose socks4 request\n302:      *\n303:      * Request format\n304:      *\n305:      *     +----+----+----+----+----+----+----+----+----+----+....+----+\n306:      *     | VN | CD | DSTPORT |      DSTIP        | USERID       |NULL|\n307:      *     +----+----+----+----+----+----+----+----+----+----+....+----+\n308:      * # of bytes:  1    1      2              4           variable       1\n309:      */\n310: \n311:     socksreq[0] = 4; /* version (SOCKS4) */\n312:     socksreq[1] = 1; /* connect */\n313:     socksreq[2] = (unsigned char)((sx->remote_port >> 8) & 0xff); /* MSB */\n314:     socksreq[3] = (unsigned char)(sx->remote_port & 0xff);        /* LSB */\n315: \n316:     /* DNS resolve only for SOCKS4, not SOCKS4a */\n317:     if(!protocol4a) {\n318:       enum resolve_t rc =\n319:         Curl_resolv(data, sx->hostname, sx->remote_port, TRUE, &dns);\n320: \n321:       if(rc == CURLRESOLV_ERROR)\n322:         return CURLPX_RESOLVE_HOST;\n323:       else if(rc == CURLRESOLV_PENDING) {\n324:         sxstate(sx, data, CONNECT_RESOLVING);\n325:         infof(data, \"SOCKS4 non-blocking resolve of %s\", sx->hostname);\n326:         return CURLPX_OK;\n327:       }\n328:       sxstate(sx, data, CONNECT_RESOLVED);\n329:       goto CONNECT_RESOLVED;\n330:     }\n331: \n332:     /* socks4a doesn't resolve anything locally */\n333:     sxstate(sx, data, CONNECT_REQ_INIT);\n334:     goto CONNECT_REQ_INIT;\n335: \n336:   case CONNECT_RESOLVING:\n337:     /* check if we have the name resolved by now */\n338:     dns = Curl_fetch_addr(data, sx->hostname, (int)conn->port);\n339: \n340:     if(dns) {\n341: #ifdef CURLRES_ASYNCH\n342:       data->state.async.dns = dns;\n343:       data->state.async.done = TRUE;\n344: #endif\n345:       infof(data, \"Hostname '%s' was found\", sx->hostname);\n346:       sxstate(sx, data, CONNECT_RESOLVED);\n347:     }\n348:     else {\n349:       result = Curl_resolv_check(data, &dns);\n350:       if(!dns) {\n351:         if(result)\n352:           return CURLPX_RESOLVE_HOST;\n353:         return CURLPX_OK;\n354:       }\n355:     }\n356:     /* FALLTHROUGH */\n357: CONNECT_RESOLVED:\n358:   case CONNECT_RESOLVED: {\n359:     struct Curl_addrinfo *hp = NULL;\n360:     /*\n361:      * We cannot use 'hostent' as a struct that Curl_resolv() returns.  It\n362:      * returns a Curl_addrinfo pointer that may not always look the same.\n363:      */\n364:     if(dns) {\n365:       hp = dns->addr;\n366: \n367:       /* scan for the first IPv4 address */\n368:       while(hp && (hp->ai_family != AF_INET))\n369:         hp = hp->ai_next;\n370: \n371:       if(hp) {\n372:         struct sockaddr_in *saddr_in;\n373:         char buf[64];\n374:         Curl_printable_address(hp, buf, sizeof(buf));\n375: \n376:         saddr_in = (struct sockaddr_in *)(void *)hp->ai_addr;\n377:         socksreq[4] = ((unsigned char *)&saddr_in->sin_addr.s_addr)[0];\n378:         socksreq[5] = ((unsigned char *)&saddr_in->sin_addr.s_addr)[1];\n379:         socksreq[6] = ((unsigned char *)&saddr_in->sin_addr.s_addr)[2];\n380:         socksreq[7] = ((unsigned char *)&saddr_in->sin_addr.s_addr)[3];\n381: \n382:         infof(data, \"SOCKS4 connect to IPv4 %s (locally resolved)\", buf);\n383: \n384:         Curl_resolv_unlock(data, dns); /* not used anymore from now on */\n385:       }\n386:       else\n387:         failf(data, \"SOCKS4 connection to %s not supported\", sx->hostname);\n388:     }\n389:     else\n390:       failf(data, \"Failed to resolve \\\"%s\\\" for SOCKS4 connect.\",\n391:             sx->hostname);\n392: \n393:     if(!hp)\n394:       return CURLPX_RESOLVE_HOST;\n395:   }\n396:     /* FALLTHROUGH */\n397: CONNECT_REQ_INIT:\n398:   case CONNECT_REQ_INIT:\n399:     /*\n400:      * This is currently not supporting \"Identification Protocol (RFC1413)\".\n401:      */\n402:     socksreq[8] = 0; /* ensure empty userid is NUL-terminated */\n403:     if(sx->proxy_user) {\n404:       size_t plen = strlen(sx->proxy_user);\n405:       if(plen >= (size_t)data->set.buffer_size - 8) {\n406:         failf(data, \"Too long SOCKS proxy user name, can't use\");\n407:         return CURLPX_LONG_USER;\n408:       }\n409:       /* copy the proxy name WITH trailing zero */\n410:       memcpy(socksreq + 8, sx->proxy_user, plen + 1);\n411:     }\n412: \n413:     /*\n414:      * Make connection\n415:      */\n416:     {\n417:       size_t packetsize = 9 +\n418:         strlen((char *)socksreq + 8); /* size including NUL */\n419: \n420:       /* If SOCKS4a, set special invalid IP address 0.0.0.x */\n421:       if(protocol4a) {\n422:         size_t hostnamelen = 0;\n423:         socksreq[4] = 0;\n424:         socksreq[5] = 0;\n425:         socksreq[6] = 0;\n426:         socksreq[7] = 1;\n427:         /* append hostname */\n428:         hostnamelen = strlen(sx->hostname) + 1; /* length including NUL */\n429:         if(hostnamelen <= 255)\n430:           strcpy((char *)socksreq + packetsize, sx->hostname);\n431:         else {\n432:           failf(data, \"SOCKS4: too long host name\");\n433:           return CURLPX_LONG_HOSTNAME;\n434:         }\n435:         packetsize += hostnamelen;\n436:       }\n437:       sx->outp = socksreq;\n438:       sx->outstanding = packetsize;\n439:       sxstate(sx, data, CONNECT_REQ_SENDING);\n440:     }\n441:     /* FALLTHROUGH */\n442:   case CONNECT_REQ_SENDING:\n443:     /* Send request */\n444:     presult = socks_state_send(cf, sx, data, CURLPX_SEND_CONNECT,\n445:                                \"SOCKS4 connect request\");\n446:     if(CURLPX_OK != presult)\n447:       return presult;\n448:     else if(sx->outstanding) {\n449:       /* remain in sending state */\n450:       return CURLPX_OK;\n451:     }\n452:     /* done sending! */\n453:     sx->outstanding = 8; /* receive data size */\n454:     sx->outp = socksreq;\n455:     sxstate(sx, data, CONNECT_SOCKS_READ);\n456: \n457:     /* FALLTHROUGH */\n458:   case CONNECT_SOCKS_READ:\n459:     /* Receive response */\n460:     presult = socks_state_recv(cf, sx, data, CURLPX_RECV_CONNECT,\n461:                                \"connect request ack\");\n462:     if(CURLPX_OK != presult)\n463:       return presult;\n464:     else if(sx->outstanding) {\n465:       /* remain in reading state */\n466:       return CURLPX_OK;\n467:     }\n468:     sxstate(sx, data, CONNECT_DONE);\n469:     break;\n470:   default: /* lots of unused states in SOCKS4 */\n471:     break;\n472:   }\n473: \n474:   /*\n475:    * Response format\n476:    *\n477:    *     +----+----+----+----+----+----+----+----+\n478:    *     | VN | CD | DSTPORT |      DSTIP        |\n479:    *     +----+----+----+----+----+----+----+----+\n480:    * # of bytes:  1    1      2              4\n481:    *\n482:    * VN is the version of the reply code and should be 0. CD is the result\n483:    * code with one of the following values:\n484:    *\n485:    * 90: request granted\n486:    * 91: request rejected or failed\n487:    * 92: request rejected because SOCKS server cannot connect to\n488:    *     identd on the client\n489:    * 93: request rejected because the client program and identd\n490:    *     report different user-ids\n491:    */\n492: \n493:   /* wrong version ? */\n494:   if(socksreq[0]) {\n495:     failf(data,\n496:           \"SOCKS4 reply has wrong version, version should be 0.\");\n497:     return CURLPX_BAD_VERSION;\n498:   }\n499: \n500:   /* Result */\n501:   switch(socksreq[1]) {\n502:   case 90:\n503:     infof(data, \"SOCKS4%s request granted.\", protocol4a?\"a\":\"\");\n504:     break;\n505:   case 91:\n506:     failf(data,\n507:           \"Can't complete SOCKS4 connection to %d.%d.%d.%d:%d. (%d)\"\n508:           \", request rejected or failed.\",\n509:           socksreq[4], socksreq[5], socksreq[6], socksreq[7],\n510:           (((unsigned char)socksreq[2] << 8) | (unsigned char)socksreq[3]),\n511:           (unsigned char)socksreq[1]);\n512:     return CURLPX_REQUEST_FAILED;\n513:   case 92:\n514:     failf(data,\n515:           \"Can't complete SOCKS4 connection to %d.%d.%d.%d:%d. (%d)\"\n516:           \", request rejected because SOCKS server cannot connect to \"\n517:           \"identd on the client.\",\n518:           socksreq[4], socksreq[5], socksreq[6], socksreq[7],\n519:           (((unsigned char)socksreq[2] << 8) | (unsigned char)socksreq[3]),\n520:           (unsigned char)socksreq[1]);\n521:     return CURLPX_IDENTD;\n522:   case 93:\n523:     failf(data,\n524:           \"Can't complete SOCKS4 connection to %d.%d.%d.%d:%d. (%d)\"\n525:           \", request rejected because the client program and identd \"\n526:           \"report different user-ids.\",\n527:           socksreq[4], socksreq[5], socksreq[6], socksreq[7],\n528:           (((unsigned char)socksreq[2] << 8) | (unsigned char)socksreq[3]),\n529:           (unsigned char)socksreq[1]);\n530:     return CURLPX_IDENTD_DIFFER;\n531:   default:\n532:     failf(data,\n533:           \"Can't complete SOCKS4 connection to %d.%d.%d.%d:%d. (%d)\"\n534:           \", Unknown.\",\n535:           socksreq[4], socksreq[5], socksreq[6], socksreq[7],\n536:           (((unsigned char)socksreq[2] << 8) | (unsigned char)socksreq[3]),\n537:           (unsigned char)socksreq[1]);\n538:     return CURLPX_UNKNOWN_FAIL;\n539:   }\n540: \n541:   return CURLPX_OK; /* Proxy was successful! */\n542: }\n543: \n544: /*\n545:  * This function logs in to a SOCKS5 proxy and sends the specifics to the final\n546:  * destination server.\n547:  */\n548: static CURLproxycode do_SOCKS5(struct Curl_cfilter *cf,\n549:                                struct socks_state *sx,\n550:                                struct Curl_easy *data)\n551: {\n552:   /*\n553:     According to the RFC1928, section \"6.  Replies\". This is what a SOCK5\n554:     replies:\n555: \n556:         +----+-----+-------+------+----------+----------+\n557:         |VER | REP |  RSV  | ATYP | BND.ADDR | BND.PORT |\n558:         +----+-----+-------+------+----------+----------+\n559:         | 1  |  1  | X'00' |  1   | Variable |    2     |\n560:         +----+-----+-------+------+----------+----------+\n561: \n562:     Where:\n563: \n564:     o  VER    protocol version: X'05'\n565:     o  REP    Reply field:\n566:     o  X'00' succeeded\n567:   */\n568:   struct connectdata *conn = cf->conn;\n569:   unsigned char *socksreq = (unsigned char *)data->state.buffer;\n570:   int idx;\n571:   CURLcode result;\n572:   CURLproxycode presult;\n573:   bool socks5_resolve_local =\n574:     (conn->socks_proxy.proxytype == CURLPROXY_SOCKS5) ? TRUE : FALSE;\n575:   const size_t hostname_len = strlen(sx->hostname);\n576:   ssize_t len = 0;\n577:   const unsigned char auth = data->set.socks5auth;\n578:   bool allow_gssapi = FALSE;\n579:   struct Curl_dns_entry *dns = NULL;\n580: \n581:   DEBUGASSERT(auth & (CURLAUTH_BASIC | CURLAUTH_GSSAPI));\n582:   switch(sx->state) {\n583:   case CONNECT_SOCKS_INIT:\n584:     if(conn->bits.httpproxy)\n585:       infof(data, \"SOCKS5: connecting to HTTP proxy %s port %d\",\n586:             sx->hostname, sx->remote_port);\n587: \n588:     /* RFC1928 chapter 5 specifies max 255 chars for domain name in packet */\n589:     if(!socks5_resolve_local && hostname_len > 255) {\n590:       infof(data, \"SOCKS5: server resolving disabled for hostnames of \"\n591:             \"length > 255 [actual len=%zu]\", hostname_len);\n592:       socks5_resolve_local = TRUE;\n593:     }\n594: \n595:     if(auth & ~(CURLAUTH_BASIC | CURLAUTH_GSSAPI))\n596:       infof(data,\n597:             \"warning: unsupported value passed to CURLOPT_SOCKS5_AUTH: %u\",\n598:             auth);\n599:     if(!(auth & CURLAUTH_BASIC))\n600:       /* disable username/password auth */\n601:       sx->proxy_user = NULL;\n602: #if defined(HAVE_GSSAPI) || defined(USE_WINDOWS_SSPI)\n603:     if(auth & CURLAUTH_GSSAPI)\n604:       allow_gssapi = TRUE;\n605: #endif\n606: \n607:     idx = 0;\n608:     socksreq[idx++] = 5;   /* version */\n609:     idx++;                 /* number of authentication methods */\n610:     socksreq[idx++] = 0;   /* no authentication */\n611:     if(allow_gssapi)\n612:       socksreq[idx++] = 1; /* GSS-API */\n613:     if(sx->proxy_user)\n614:       socksreq[idx++] = 2; /* username/password */\n615:     /* write the number of authentication methods */\n616:     socksreq[1] = (unsigned char) (idx - 2);\n617: \n618:     sx->outp = socksreq;\n619:     sx->outstanding = idx;\n620:     presult = socks_state_send(cf, sx, data, CURLPX_SEND_CONNECT,\n621:                                \"initial SOCKS5 request\");\n622:     if(CURLPX_OK != presult)\n623:       return presult;\n624:     else if(sx->outstanding) {\n625:       /* remain in sending state */\n626:       return CURLPX_OK;\n627:     }\n628:     sxstate(sx, data, CONNECT_SOCKS_READ);\n629:     goto CONNECT_SOCKS_READ_INIT;\n630:   case CONNECT_SOCKS_SEND:\n631:     presult = socks_state_send(cf, sx, data, CURLPX_SEND_CONNECT,\n632:                                \"initial SOCKS5 request\");\n633:     if(CURLPX_OK != presult)\n634:       return presult;\n635:     else if(sx->outstanding) {\n636:       /* remain in sending state */\n637:       return CURLPX_OK;\n638:     }\n639:     /* FALLTHROUGH */\n640: CONNECT_SOCKS_READ_INIT:\n641:   case CONNECT_SOCKS_READ_INIT:\n642:     sx->outstanding = 2; /* expect two bytes */\n643:     sx->outp = socksreq; /* store it here */\n644:     /* FALLTHROUGH */\n645:   case CONNECT_SOCKS_READ:\n646:     presult = socks_state_recv(cf, sx, data, CURLPX_RECV_CONNECT,\n647:                                \"initial SOCKS5 response\");\n648:     if(CURLPX_OK != presult)\n649:       return presult;\n650:     else if(sx->outstanding) {\n651:       /* remain in reading state */\n652:       return CURLPX_OK;\n653:     }\n654:     else if(socksreq[0] != 5) {\n655:       failf(data, \"Received invalid version in initial SOCKS5 response.\");\n656:       return CURLPX_BAD_VERSION;\n657:     }\n658:     else if(socksreq[1] == 0) {\n659:       /* DONE! No authentication needed. Send request. */\n660:       sxstate(sx, data, CONNECT_REQ_INIT);\n661:       goto CONNECT_REQ_INIT;\n662:     }\n663:     else if(socksreq[1] == 2) {\n664:       /* regular name + password authentication */\n665:       sxstate(sx, data, CONNECT_AUTH_INIT);\n666:       goto CONNECT_AUTH_INIT;\n667:     }\n668: #if defined(HAVE_GSSAPI) || defined(USE_WINDOWS_SSPI)\n669:     else if(allow_gssapi && (socksreq[1] == 1)) {\n670:       sxstate(sx, data, CONNECT_GSSAPI_INIT);\n671:       result = Curl_SOCKS5_gssapi_negotiate(cf, data);\n672:       if(result) {\n673:         failf(data, \"Unable to negotiate SOCKS5 GSS-API context.\");\n674:         return CURLPX_GSSAPI;\n675:       }\n676:     }\n677: #endif\n678:     else {\n679:       /* error */\n680:       if(!allow_gssapi && (socksreq[1] == 1)) {\n681:         failf(data,\n682:               \"SOCKS5 GSSAPI per-message authentication is not supported.\");\n683:         return CURLPX_GSSAPI_PERMSG;\n684:       }\n685:       else if(socksreq[1] == 255) {\n686:         failf(data, \"No authentication method was acceptable.\");\n687:         return CURLPX_NO_AUTH;\n688:       }\n689:     }\n690:     failf(data,\n691:           \"Undocumented SOCKS5 mode attempted to be used by server.\");\n692:     return CURLPX_UNKNOWN_MODE;\n693: #if defined(HAVE_GSSAPI) || defined(USE_WINDOWS_SSPI)\n694:   case CONNECT_GSSAPI_INIT:\n695:     /* GSSAPI stuff done non-blocking */\n696:     break;\n697: #endif\n698: \n699:   default: /* do nothing! */\n700:     break;\n701: \n702: CONNECT_AUTH_INIT:\n703:   case CONNECT_AUTH_INIT: {\n704:     /* Needs user name and password */\n705:     size_t proxy_user_len, proxy_password_len;\n706:     if(sx->proxy_user && sx->proxy_password) {\n707:       proxy_user_len = strlen(sx->proxy_user);\n708:       proxy_password_len = strlen(sx->proxy_password);\n709:     }\n710:     else {\n711:       proxy_user_len = When a user configures curl to use a SOCKS5 proxy, the function processes responses from the proxy server, making it directly exposed to attacker-controlled data. The attack vector is configuring curl with a malicious or attacker-controlled SOCKS5 proxy server.\n\n---\n\n## Affected Code\n\n**Function:** `do_SOCKS5()`\n**File:** `lib/socks.c` (lines 548-1054)\n**Type:** Static function that implements SOCKS5 proxy protocol handshake\n\n**Description:** This function handles the complete SOCKS5 proxy negotiation sequence, including:\n- Initial handshake with the proxy server\n- Authentication mechanism negotiation (GSSAPI, username/password, or none)\n- Username/password authentication if selected\n- CONNECT request to establish tunnel to remote host\n- Processing SOCKS5 responses and error codes\n\n---\n\n## Attack Path\n\n### Complete Call Chain from Entry Point to do_SOCKS5()\n\n```\nmain() / curl_easy_perform()\n  ↓\nCurl_connect() [lib/url.c:3895]\n  ↓\nCurl_setup_conn() [lib/url.c:3858]\n  ↓\nCurl_conn_setup() [lib/connect.c:1416]\n  ↓\ncf_setup_add() [lib/connect.c:1364]\n  ↓\ncf_setup_connect() [lib/connect.c:1186]\n  ↓ (checks: ctx->state < CF_SETUP_CNNCT_SOCKS && cf->conn->bits.socksproxy)\n  ↓\nCurl_cf_socks_proxy_insert_after() [lib/socks.c:1240]\n  ↓\nsocks_proxy_cf_connect() [lib/socks.c:1103]\n  ↓\nconnect_SOCKS() [lib/socks.c:1056]\n  ↓ (switch: conn->socks_proxy.proxytype == CURLPROXY_SOCKS5*)\n  ↓\ndo_SOCKS5() [lib/socks.c:548]\n```\n\n### Function Roles in the Chain\n\n1. **main() / curl_easy_perform()** - Entry point: User initiates curl transfer\n2. **Curl_connect()** - Main connection orchestrator, calls DNS resolution\n3. **Curl_setup_conn()** - Post-DNS setup, initiates filter chain creation\n4. **Curl_conn_setup()** - Creates the root setup filter\n5. **cf_setup_add()** - Adds setup filter to connection chain\n6. **cf_setup_connect()** - Connection filter callback that checks proxy configuration\n   - **Critical check:** `if(ctx->state < CF_SETUP_CNNCT_SOCKS && cf->conn->bits.socksproxy)`\n   - Decides whether to insert SOCKS proxy filter based on user configuration\n7. **Curl_cf_socks_proxy_insert_after()** - Inserts SOCKS proxy filter into chain\n8. **socks_proxy_cf_connect()** - SOCKS proxy filter's connection callback\n9. **connect_SOCKS()** - State machine dispatcher for SOCKS protocol\n10. **do_SOCKS5()** - Implements SOCKS5-specific state machine handling\n\n### Source of External Input\n\nThe `bits.socksproxy` flag is set in `lib/url.c:1547` based on user-provided proxy configuration:\n\n```c\nconn->bits.socksproxy = (conn->bits.proxy &&\n                         !conn->bits.httpproxy) ? TRUE : FALSE;\n```\n\nThe proxy configuration comes from:\n- `--proxy` command-line flag\n- Environment variables (http_proxy, https_proxy, etc.)\n- User code via `CURLOPT_PROXY` option\n\n---\n\n## Severity Assessment\n\n### Reachability: **YES - FULLY REACHABLE**\n\nThe function is directly reachable from external attacker-controlled input when a user configures a SOCKS5 proxy.\n\n### Attack Vector: **Attacker-Controlled SOCKS5 Proxy Server**\n\nTo trigger code execution or exploitation of `do_SOCKS5()`:\n\n1. **User Action Required:** User must configure curl to use a SOCKS5 proxy:\n   ```bash\n   curl https://example.com --proxy socks5://attacker-proxy:1080\n   ```\n\n2. **Attack Execution:** The attacker controls the SOCKS5 proxy server listening on port 1080 (or configured port)\n\n3. **Attack Triggers:** Attacker sends malformed or crafted SOCKS5 responses when:\n   - Curl sends initial SOCKS5 greeting\n   - Curl sends CONNECT request with destination hostname\n   - Curl awaits proxy responses during authentication and connection establishment\n\n### External Input to do_SOCKS5()\n\nAll of the following data originates from the attacker-controlled proxy server:\n\n1. **SOCKS5 Response Bytes:**\n   - `socksreq[0]` - Protocol version (should be 5)\n   - `socksreq[1]` - Authentication method selected\n   - `socksreq[3]` - Address type in CONNECT response\n   - `socksreq[4]` - Domain name length / IPv6 address data\n   - Authentication response codes\n\n2. **Attack Scenarios:**\n   - **Stack overflow:** Hostname length field (`socksreq[4]` at line 1007) is not bounds-checked in CONNECT response processing\n   - **Out-of-bounds read:** Domain name parsing (line 1005-1008) uses user-controlled length\n   - **Integer overflow:** Port number, hostname length calculations\n   - **Logic errors:** Misinterpretation of response codes leading to false success\n\n### Exploitation Requirements\n\n| Component | Requirement |\n|-----------|-------------|\n| **User Configuration** | Must specify `--proxy socks5://attacker:port` |\n| **Network Access** | Attacker must be able to accept connections and send SOCKS5 responses |\n| **Victim Vulnerability** | Vulnerable curl version with bugs in SOCKS5 parsing |\n| **Impact** | RCE, memory corruption, information disclosure |\n\n### Risk Factors\n\n- **High Reachability:** Any user using SOCKS5 proxies is vulnerable\n- **User Control:** Users explicitly specify the proxy address\n- **Attack Complexity:** Medium - attacker needs control of proxy server or MitM position\n- **Impact Potential:** High - reaches network protocol parsing code processing untrusted data\n\n---\n\n## Remediation\n\n### Input Validation Issues\n\nThe `do_SOCKS5()` function processes the following potentially dangerous fields:\n\n#### 1. **Domain Name Length Field (Line 1007)**\n```c\nif(socksreq[3] == 3) {\n  /* domain name */\n  int addrlen = (int) socksreq[4];  // ⚠️ UNTRUSTED LENGTH\n  len = 5 + addrlen + 2;\n}\n```\n\n**Recommendation:** Add bounds checking:\n```c\nif(socksreq[3] == 3) {\n  int addrlen = (int) socksreq[4];\n  if(addrlen > 255 || (5 + addrlen + 2) > READBUFFER_MIN) {\n    failf(data, \"SOCKS5 domain name length exceeds buffer\");\n    return CURLPX_BAD_ADDRESS_TYPE;\n  }\n  len = 5 + addrlen + 2;\n}\n```\n\n#### 2. **Hostname Length Validation (Line 589)**\n```c\nif(!socks5_resolve_local && hostname_len > 255) {\n  // ✓ Good: Already validated\n}\n```\n\n#### 3. **Buffer Overflow in Hostname Encoding (Line 906)**\n```c\nsocksreq[len++] = (char) hostname_len; // ⚠️ Direct cast without range check\nmemcpy(&socksreq[len], sx->hostname, hostname_len);\n```\n\n**Recommendation:** Validate hostname_len before use:\n```c\nif(hostname_len > 255) {\n  failf(data, \"hostname too long for SOCKS5\");\n  return CURLPX_LONG_HOSTNAME;\n}\nsocksreq[len++] = (unsigned char) hostname_len;\n```\n\n#### 4. **Response Code Processing (Line 965)**\n```c\nelse if(socksreq[1]) { /* Anything besides 0 is an error */\n  // Handles error responses, but validates...\n  if(code < 9) {\n    // Uses lookup table (good bounds check)\n  }\n}\n```\n\n**Status:** Reasonably protected with lookup table\n\n### Overall Risk Assessment\n\n**Current State:** The function has some protections but also vulnerable areas:\n- ✓ Proxy user/password lengths are validated (lines 727, 737)\n- ✓ Error codes are bounds-checked with lookup table\n- ⚠️ Domain name length field from proxy response lacks validation\n- ⚠️ Hostname parameter validation exists but could be stricter\n\n**Priority Fixes:**\n1. Validate domain name length from proxy response before calculating buffer offset\n2. Add comprehensive bounds checking for all proxy response fields\n3. Use size_t for all length calculations to prevent integer overflow\n4. Implement assertions for buffer boundaries\n\n---\n\n## Conclusion\n\nThe `do_SOCKS5()` function **IS REACHABLE** from attacker-controlled input via a malicious SOCKS5 proxy server. The attack vector requires user configuration of a SOCKS5 proxy, but once configured, all response data from the proxy flows directly into this function with limited validation.\n\n**Risk Level:** MEDIUM-HIGH for users configuring SOCKS5 proxies\n\n**Affected Scenarios:**\n- Corporate environments using SOCKS5 proxies\n- Tor network users (uses SOCKS5)\n- Users behind SOCKS proxies for privacy\n- Any configuration with `curl --proxy socks5://`\n"},"caller":{"type":"direct"}}],"stop_reason":null,"stop_sequence":null,"usage":{"input_tokens":9,"cache_creation_input_tokens":1805,"cache_read_input_tokens":79894,"cache_creation":{"ephemeral_5m_input_tokens":0,"ephemeral_1h_input_tokens":1805},"output_tokens":1,"service_tier":"standard","inference_geo":"not_available"},"context_management":null},"parent_tool_use_id":null,"session_id":"96c18f90-354d-4fe5-930b-8e32726419ea","uuid":"c4fe43cd-69d1-43d4-bf07-e9524adbc54b"}
